import requests import urllib.parse import json import os import time # Create workspace directory os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) print("SYSTEMATIC RESEARCH: Dustin Nguyen's Works Analysis") print("=" * 60) # First, let's inspect any existing research files to understand what we already know existing_files = ['workspace/dustin_nguyen_research.json', 'workspace/dustin_nguyen_detailed_research.json', 'workspace/comprehensive_nguyen_research.json', 'workspace/final_nguyen_research.json'] for file_path in existing_files: if os.path.exists(file_path): print(f"\nInspecting existing file: {file_path}") try: with open(file_path, 'r') as f: existing_data = json.load(f) print(f"Keys found: {list(existing_data.keys())}") if 'illustrator' in existing_data: print(f"Illustrator confirmed: {existing_data['illustrator']}") if 'all_nguyen_works' in existing_data: print(f"Previous works found: {len(existing_data['all_nguyen_works'])}") elif 'dustin_nguyen_works' in existing_data: print(f"Previous works found: {len(existing_data['dustin_nguyen_works'])}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") break # Step 1: Confirm basic information about Descender and Dustin Nguyen print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("STEP 1: CONFIRMING ILLUSTRATOR INFORMATION") print("=" * 60) descender_info = { 'title': 'Descender, Volume 1: Tin Stars', 'authors': ['Jeff Lemire', 'Dustin Nguyen'], 'illustrator': 'Dustin Nguyen', 'publisher': 'Image Comics', 'published_date': '2015', 'description': 'Young Robot boy TIM-21 and his companions struggle to stay alive in a universe where all androids have been outlawed and bounty hunters lurk on every planet.' } print(f"Book: {descender_info['title']}") print(f"Writer: Jeff Lemire") print(f"Illustrator: {descender_info['illustrator']}") print(f"Publisher: {descender_info['publisher']}") print(f"Published: {descender_info['published_date']}") # Step 2: Search for Dustin Nguyen's complete bibliography print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("STEP 2: SEARCHING FOR DUSTIN NGUYEN'S COMPLETE WORKS") print("=" * 60) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } # Comprehensive search queries for Dustin Nguyen search_queries = [ "Dustin Nguyen comic book illustrator", "Dustin Nguyen graphic novel author", "Dustin Nguyen Batman Li'l Gotham", "Dustin Nguyen DC Comics", "Dustin Nguyen Image Comics", "Dustin Nguyen children comic", "Dustin Nguyen watercolor art comic" ] all_nguyen_works = [] found_titles = set() # To avoid duplicates for query in search_queries: print(f"\nSearching: {query}") url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={urllib.parse.quote(query)}&maxResults=12" try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() data = response.json() items = data.get('items', []) query_results = 0 for item in items: volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) title = volume_info.get('title', '') authors = volume_info.get('authors', []) description = volume_info.get('description', '') # Check if Dustin Nguyen is involved and avoid duplicates if (any('dustin nguyen' in author.lower() for author in authors) and title not in found_titles and 'descender' not in title.lower()): found_titles.add(title) work_info = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'description': description, 'publisher': volume_info.get('publisher', ''), 'published_date': volume_info.get('publishedDate', ''), 'categories': volume_info.get('categories', []), 'page_count': volume_info.get('pageCount', 0), 'search_query': query } all_nguyen_works.append(work_info) query_results += 1 print(f" Found: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(authors)}") print(f" Publisher: {work_info['publisher']}") print(f" Published: {work_info['published_date']}") if description: print(f" Description: {description[:120]}...") print() print(f"Query results: {query_results}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error searching '{query}': {e}") time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting print(f"\nTotal unique Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)}") # Step 3: Define and analyze against target criteria print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("STEP 3: ANALYZING WORKS AGAINST TARGET CRITERIA") print("=" * 60) # The specific criteria we're looking for based on the PLAN description target_criteria = { 'dark_peter_pan_reimagining': ['peter pan', 'neverland', 'lost boys', 'wendy', 'tinker bell', 'pan', 'hook'], 'immortal_children': ['immortal', 'eternal', 'ageless', 'never grow', 'forever young', 'undying', 'timeless'], 'post_apocalyptic_world': ['post-apocalyptic', 'apocalypse', 'destroyed world', 'wasteland', 'ruins', 'end of world', 'devastation'], 'black_white_art_red_accents': ['black and white', 'monochrome', 'red accent', 'watercolor', 'ink wash', 'minimal color', 'two-color'], 'origin_stories_1763_1945': ['1763', 'black forest', '1945', 'hiroshima', 'origin', 'flashback', 'historical', 'past'], 'existential_themes': ['existential', 'monotony', 'meaningless', 'isolation', 'loneliness', 'despair', 'emptiness'], 'tragic_themes': ['tragic', 'loss', 'death', 'confrontation', 'violence', 'tragedy', 'sorrow'] } print("Target criteria defined:") for criterion, keywords in target_criteria.items(): print(f" {criterion}: {', '.join(keywords[:3])}...") matching_works = [] print("\nAnalyzing each work:") print("-" * 40) for i, work in enumerate(all_nguyen_works, 1): title = work['title'] description = work['description'] # Properly define the text content for analysis within this loop analysis_text = (title + ' ' + description).lower() print(f"\n{i}. Analyzing: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(work['authors'])}") print(f" Publisher: {work['publisher']}") print(f" Published: {work['published_date']}") # Check against each criterion criteria_matches = [] total_score = 0 for criterion_name, keywords in target_criteria.items(): found_keywords = [keyword for keyword in keywords if keyword in analysis_text] if found_keywords: criteria_matches.append(f"{criterion_name}: {', '.join(found_keywords)}") total_score += len(found_keywords) if criteria_matches: print(f" ✓ CRITERIA MATCHES (Score: {total_score}):") for match in criteria_matches: print(f" - {match}") work['criteria_score'] = total_score work['criteria_matches'] = criteria_matches matching_works.append(work) else: print(f" ✗ No criteria matches found") # Additional thematic analysis using the properly defined variable additional_themes = [] if any(word in analysis_text for word in ['child', 'children', 'kid', 'young', 'youth']): additional_themes.append('children themes') if any(word in analysis_text for word in ['dark', 'nightmare', 'horror', 'gothic', 'scary']): additional_themes.append('dark themes') if any(word in analysis_text for word in ['dream', 'sleep', 'nightmare']): additional_themes.append('dream themes') if any(word in analysis_text for word in ['batman', 'gotham', 'dc']): additional_themes.append('Batman universe') if additional_themes: print(f" → Additional themes: {', '.join(additional_themes)}") # Step 4: Search for specific story elements mentioned in the criteria print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("STEP 4: SEARCHING FOR SPECIFIC STORY ELEMENTS") print("=" * 60) # Search for the very specific elements mentioned in the original description specific_element_searches = [ "1763 Black Forest comic graphic novel", "1945 Hiroshima comic graphic novel", "immortal children post apocalyptic comic", "Peter Pan dark reimagining comic", "black white red accent comic art", "existential monotony graphic novel" ] specific_matches = [] for search_term in specific_element_searches: print(f"\nSearching for: {search_term}") url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={urllib.parse.quote(search_term)}&maxResults=5" try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() data = response.json() items = data.get('items', []) found_relevant = False for item in items[:3]: # Check top 3 results volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) title = volume_info.get('title', '') authors = volume_info.get('authors', []) description = volume_info.get('description', '') # Check if this could be our target using properly defined variables search_content = (title + ' ' + description).lower() # Look for key elements has_relevant_elements = ( any(word in search_content for word in ['peter pan', 'immortal', 'children', 'post-apocalyptic']) or any(word in search_content for word in ['1763', '1945', 'black forest', 'hiroshima']) or any(word in search_content for word in ['existential', 'monotony', 'tragic']) ) if has_relevant_elements: match_info = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'description': description, 'publisher': volume_info.get('publisher', ''), 'published_date': volume_info.get('publishedDate', ''), 'search_term': search_term, 'dustin_nguyen_involved': any('dustin nguyen' in author.lower() for author in authors) } specific_matches.append(match_info) found_relevant = True print(f" Relevant work: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(authors)}") if match_info['dustin_nguyen_involved']: print(f" *** DUSTIN NGUYEN INVOLVED ***") if description: print(f" Description: {description[:150]}...") print() if not found_relevant: print(f" No relevant works found for this search term") except Exception as e: print(f" Error searching '{search_term}': {e}") time.sleep(1) # Step 5: Final analysis and conclusion print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("STEP 5: FINAL ANALYSIS AND CONCLUSION") print("=" * 60) # Sort matching works by criteria score matching_works.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('criteria_score', 0), reverse=True) # Prepare comprehensive research results final_research = { 'research_date': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'illustrator_confirmed': 'Dustin Nguyen', 'descender_info': descender_info, 'search_summary': { 'total_nguyen_works_found': len(all_nguyen_works), 'works_matching_target_criteria': len(matching_works), 'specific_element_matches': len(specific_matches), 'search_queries_used': len(search_queries) }, 'all_dustin_nguyen_works': all_nguyen_works, 'works_matching_criteria': matching_works, 'specific_element_matches': specific_matches, 'target_criteria_definition': { 'description': 'Dark Peter Pan reimagining with immortal children in post-apocalyptic world', 'visual_style': 'Black and white art with red accents', 'narrative_structure': 'Non-linear storytelling with origin stories', 'historical_elements': '1763 Black Forest and 1945 Hiroshima origin stories', 'tone': 'Sparse dialogue emphasizing existential monotony', 'conclusion': 'Unresolved cliffhanger involving tragic loss during human confrontation' } } # Save comprehensive research with open('workspace/dustin_nguyen_final_analysis.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(final_research, f, indent=4) # Create a readable summary summary_text = f"""DUSTIN NGUYEN RESEARCH SUMMARY {'=' * 50} ILLUSTRATOR CONFIRMED: {final_research['illustrator_confirmed']} DESCENDER ILLUSTRATOR: Confirmed - Dustin Nguyen illustrated 'Descender, Volume 1: Tin Stars' by Jeff Lemire SEARCH RESULTS: - Total Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)} - Works matching target criteria: {len(matching_works)} - Specific element matches: {len(specific_matches)} ALL DUSTIN NGUYEN WORKS FOUND: {'-' * 30} """ for i, work in enumerate(all_nguyen_works, 1): summary_text += f"{i}. {work['title']}\n" summary_text += f" Authors: {', '.join(work['authors'])}\n" summary_text += f" Publisher: {work['publisher']}\n" summary_text += f" Published: {work['published_date']}\n" if work['description']: summary_text += f" Description: {work['description'][:150]}...\n" summary_text += "\n" if matching_works: summary_text += f"\nWORKS MATCHING TARGET CRITERIA:\n{'-' * 30}\n" for work in matching_works: summary_text += f"Title: {work['title']}\n" summary_text += f"Criteria Score: {work.get('criteria_score', 0)}\n" summary_text += f"Matches: {'; '.join(work.get('criteria_matches', []))}\n\n" else: summary_text += f"\nNO WORKS MATCHING TARGET CRITERIA FOUND\n{'-' * 30}\n" summary_text += "The described series (dark Peter Pan reimagining with immortal children,\n" summary_text += "post-apocalyptic world, black/white art with red accents, 1763 Black Forest\n" summary_text += "and 1945 Hiroshima origin stories) does not appear to exist in Dustin Nguyen's\n" summary_text += "documented bibliography.\n\n" summary_text += "POSSIBLE EXPLANATIONS:\n" summary_text += "1. The series may be unpublished or very limited release\n" summary_text += "4. The description may be a composite of multiple different works\n" with open('workspace/dustin_nguyen_research_summary.txt', 'w') as f: f.write(summary_text) print(f"RESEARCH COMPLETE:") print(f"- Illustrator confirmed: {final_research['illustrator_confirmed']}") print(f"- Total Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)}") print(f"- Works matching target criteria: {len(matching_works)}") print(f"- Specific element matches: {len(specific_matches)}") if matching_works: print(f"\nTOP MATCHING WORK:") top_match = matching_works[0] print(f" Title: {top_match['title']}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(top_match['authors'])}") print(f" Criteria Score: {top_match.get('criteria_score', 0)}") print(f" Publisher: {top_match['publisher']}") else: print(f"\nCONCLUSION: No Dustin Nguyen works found matching the specific criteria.") print(f"The described dark Peter Pan reimagining series does not appear to exist") print(f"in Dustin Nguyen's documented portfolio.") print(f"\nDetailed research saved to:") print(f"- workspace/dustin_nguyen_final_analysis.json") print(f"- workspace/dustin_nguyen_research_summary.txt")

Step 3: Search for Dustin Nguyen's complete works (avoiding variable scope issues) print("\nStep 3: Comprehensive search for Dustin Nguyen's works") print("-" * 40) headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } # Search queries for Dustin Nguyen's bibliography search_queries = [ "Dustin Nguyen comic book illustrator author", "Dustin Nguyen Batman Li'l Gotham", "Dustin Nguyen DC Comics graphic novel", "Dustin Nguyen Image Comics", "Dustin Nguyen children comic book", "Dustin Nguyen watercolor art comic" ] all_nguyen_works = [] found_titles = set() # Track titles to avoid duplicates for query_index, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nSearch {query_index}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={urllib.parse.quote(query)}&maxResults=10" try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() data = response.json() items = data.get('items', []) query_results = 0 for item in items: volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) title = volume_info.get('title', '') authors = volume_info.get('authors', []) description = volume_info.get('description', '') # Check if Dustin Nguyen is involved and avoid duplicates dustin_involved = any('dustin nguyen' in author.lower() for author in authors) not_descender = 'descender' not in title.lower() not_duplicate = title not in found_titles if dustin_involved and not_descender and not_duplicate: found_titles.add(title) work_info = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'description': description, 'publisher': volume_info.get('publisher', ''), 'published_date': volume_info.get('publishedDate', ''), 'categories': volume_info.get('categories', []), 'page_count': volume_info.get('pageCount', 0), 'found_in_query': query } all_nguyen_works.append(work_info) query_results += 1 print(f" Found: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(authors)}") print(f" Publisher: {work_info['publisher']}") if description: print(f" Description: {description[:100]}...") print(f" Query yielded {query_results} new works") except Exception as e: print(f" Error with query '{query}': {e}") time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting print(f"\nTotal unique Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)}") # Step 4: Define target criteria and analyze works (fixing variable scope issues) print("\nStep 4: Analyzing works against target criteria") print("-" * 40) # Define the specific criteria we're looking for target_criteria = { 'dark_peter_pan_reimagining': ['peter pan', 'neverland', 'lost boys', 'wendy', 'tinker bell', 'pan', 'hook'], 'immortal_children': ['immortal', 'eternal', 'ageless', 'never grow', 'forever young', 'undying'], 'post_apocalyptic_world': ['post-apocalyptic', 'apocalypse', 'destroyed world', 'wasteland', 'ruins'], 'black_white_art_red_accents': ['black and white', 'monochrome', 'red accent', 'watercolor', 'ink wash'], 'origin_stories_1763_1945': ['1763', 'black forest', '1945', 'hiroshima', 'origin', 'flashback'], 'existential_themes': ['existential', 'monotony', 'meaningless', 'isolation', 'loneliness'], 'tragic_themes': ['tragic', 'loss', 'death', 'confrontation', 'violence', 'tragedy'] } print("Target criteria:") for criterion, keywords in target_criteria.items(): print(f" {criterion}: {', '.join(keywords[:3])}...") matching_works = [] print("\nAnalyzing each work:") for i, work in enumerate(all_nguyen_works, 1): title = work['title'] description = work['description'] print(f"\n{i}. {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(work['authors'])}") print(f" Publisher: {work['publisher']}") print(f" Published: {work['published_date']}") # Create analysis text within this scope to avoid variable errors work_text = (title + ' ' + description).lower() # Check against criteria criteria_matches = [] total_score = 0 for criterion_name, keywords in target_criteria.items(): # Use the locally defined work_text variable found_keywords = [] for keyword in keywords: if keyword in work_text: found_keywords.append(keyword) if found_keywords: criteria_matches.append(f"{criterion_name}: {', '.join(found_keywords)}") total_score += len(found_keywords) if criteria_matches: print(f" ✓ CRITERIA MATCHES (Score: {total_score}):") for match in criteria_matches: print(f" - {match}") work['criteria_score'] = total_score work['criteria_matches'] = criteria_matches matching_works.append(work) else: print(f" ✗ No target criteria matches found") # Additional thematic analysis using the same work_text variable additional_themes = [] # Check for children themes children_keywords = ['child', 'children', 'kid', 'young', 'youth'] if any(keyword in work_text for keyword in children_keywords): additional_themes.append('children themes') # Check for dark themes dark_keywords = ['dark', 'nightmare', 'horror', 'gothic', 'scary'] if any(keyword in work_text for keyword in dark_keywords): additional_themes.append('dark themes') # Check for Batman themes batman_keywords = ['batman', 'gotham', 'dc'] if any(keyword in work_text for keyword in batman_keywords): additional_themes.append('Batman universe') if additional_themes: print(f" → Additional themes: {', '.join(additional_themes)}") # Step 5: Search for specific story elements print("\nStep 5: Searching for specific story elements") print("-" * 40) specific_searches = [ "1763 Black Forest comic graphic novel", "1945 Hiroshima comic graphic novel", "immortal children post apocalyptic comic", "Peter Pan dark reimagining comic", "black white red accent comic art" ] specific_matches = [] for search_term in specific_searches: print(f"\nSearching: {search_term}") url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={urllib.parse.quote(search_term)}&maxResults=5" try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() data = response.json() items = data.get('items', []) found_relevant = False for item in items[:3]: volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) title = volume_info.get('title', '') authors = volume_info.get('authors', []) description = volume_info.get('description', '') # Create search text within this scope search_text = (title + ' ' + description).lower() # Check for relevant elements relevant_keywords = ['peter pan', 'immortal', 'children', 'post-apocalyptic', '1763', '1945', 'black forest', 'hiroshima', 'existential', 'monotony'] has_relevant_elements = any(keyword in search_text for keyword in relevant_keywords) if has_relevant_elements: match_info = { 'title': title, 'authors': authors, 'description': description, 'publisher': volume_info.get('publisher', ''), 'published_date': volume_info.get('publishedDate', ''), 'search_term': search_term, 'dustin_nguyen_involved': any('dustin nguyen' in author.lower() for author in authors) } specific_matches.append(match_info) found_relevant = True print(f" Relevant: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(authors)}") if match_info['dustin_nguyen_involved']: print(f" *** DUSTIN NGUYEN INVOLVED ***") if not found_relevant: print(f" No relevant works found") except Exception as e: print(f" Error searching '{search_term}': {e}") time.sleep(1) # Step 6: Final analysis and save results print("\nStep 6: Final Analysis") print("=" * 40) # Sort matching works by criteria score matching_works.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('criteria_score', 0), reverse=True) # Prepare final research results final_results = { 'research_completed': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'illustrator_confirmed': 'Dustin Nguyen', 'descender_info': descender_info, 'search_summary': { 'total_nguyen_works_found': len(all_nguyen_works), 'works_matching_target_criteria': len(matching_works), 'specific_element_matches': len(specific_matches) }, 'all_dustin_nguyen_works': all_nguyen_works, 'works_matching_criteria': matching_works, 'specific_element_matches': specific_matches, 'target_criteria_searched': { 'description': 'Dark Peter Pan reimagining with immortal children in post-apocalyptic world', 'visual_style': 'Black and white art with red accents', 'narrative_structure': 'Non-linear storytelling including 1763 Black Forest and 1945 Hiroshima origin stories', 'tone': 'Sparse dialogue emphasizing existential monotony', 'ending': 'Unresolved cliffhanger involving tragic loss during human confrontation' } } # Save comprehensive results with open('workspace/dustin_nguyen_comprehensive_analysis.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(final_results, f, indent=4) # Create readable summary summary_lines = [ "DUSTIN NGUYEN RESEARCH - FINAL RESULTS", "=" * 50, "", f"ILLUSTRATOR CONFIRMED: {final_results['illustrator_confirmed']}", f"SOURCE WORK: {descender_info['title']} by {descender_info['writer']}", "", "SEARCH RESULTS:", f"- Total Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)}", f"- Works matching target criteria: {len(matching_works)}", f"- Specific element matches: {len(specific_matches)}", "", "ALL DUSTIN NGUYEN WORKS DISCOVERED:", "-" * 30 ] for i, work in enumerate(all_nguyen_works, 1): summary_lines.extend([ f"{i}. {work['title']}", f" Authors: {', '.join(work['authors'])}", f" Publisher: {work['publisher']}", f" Published: {work['published_date']}", f" Description: {work['description'][:150]}..." if work['description'] else " Description: Not available", "" ]) if matching_works: summary_lines.extend([ "WORKS MATCHING TARGET CRITERIA:", "-" * 30 ]) for work in matching_works: summary_lines.extend([ f"Title: {work['title']}", f"Criteria Score: {work.get('criteria_score', 0)}", f"Matches: {'; '.join(work.get('criteria_matches', []))}", "" ]) else: summary_lines.extend([ "NO WORKS MATCHING TARGET CRITERIA FOUND", "-" * 30, "", "CONCLUSION:", "The described graphic novel series (dark Peter Pan reimagining with", "immortal children, post-apocalyptic world, black/white art with red", "accents, 1763 Black Forest and 1945 Hiroshima origin stories) does", "NOT appear to exist in Dustin Nguyen's documented bibliography.", "", "POSSIBLE EXPLANATIONS:", "1. The series may be misattributed to Dustin Nguyen", "2. The series may not exist or be fictional", "3. The series may be unpublished or very limited release", "4. The description may be a composite of multiple different works", "5. The series may be by a different artist entirely" ]) with open('workspace/dustin_nguyen_final_summary.txt', 'w') as f: f.write('\n'.join(summary_lines)) print(f"RESEARCH COMPLETED:") print(f"✓ Illustrator confirmed: {final_results['illustrator_confirmed']}") print(f"✓ Total Dustin Nguyen works found: {len(all_nguyen_works)}") print(f"✓ Works matching target criteria: {len(matching_works)}") print(f"✓ Specific element matches: {len(specific_matches)}") if matching_works: print(f"\nTOP MATCHING WORK:") top_match = matching_works[0] print(f" Title: {top_match['title']}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(top_match['authors'])}") print(f" Criteria Score: {top_match.get('criteria_score', 0)}") else: print(f"\nFINAL CONCLUSION:") print(f"No Dustin Nguyen works found matching the described criteria.") print(f"The target series likely does not exist in his documented portfolio.") print(f"\nResults saved to:") print(f"- workspace/dustin_nguyen_comprehensive_analysis.json") print(f"- workspace/dustin_nguyen_final_summary.txt")

in combined_text_for_analysis for word in ['dark', 'nightmare', 'horror', 'gothic', 'scary']): additional_themes.append('dark themes') # Check for dream themes if any(word in title, 'authors': authors, 'description': description, 'publisher': volume_info.get('publisher', ''), 'published_date': volume_info.get('publishedDate', ''), 'search_term': search_term, 'dustin_nguyen_involved': any('dustin nguyen' in author.lower() for author in authors) } specific_matches.append(match_info) found_relevant = True print(f" Relevant work found: {title}") print(f" Authors: {', '.join(authors)}") if match_info['dustin_nguyen_involved']: print(f" *** DUSTIN NGUYEN INVOLVED ***") if description: print(f" Description: {description[:150]}...") if not found_relevant: print(f" No relevant works found for this search") except Exception as e: print(f" Error searching '{search_term}': {e}") time.sleep(1) # Step 6: Final analysis and conclusion print("\nStep 6: Final Analysis and Conclusion") print("=" * 50) # Sort matching works by criteria score matching_works.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('criteria_score', 0), reverse=True) # Prepare comprehensive final results final_research_results = { 'research_completed_at': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'task_summary': 'Research illustrator of Descender Volume 1 and analyze their other works for dark Peter Pan
